prospect_for_resources = {
	
	algeria_oil_wells = { #514
		
		icon = oil

		# allowed = {

		# }

		available = {
			owns_state = 514
			controls_state = 514
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2
			has_tech = excavation6
		}

		
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 514
			}
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 514
			controls_state = 514
			514 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = algeria_oil_wells_completed_1
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 120

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}

		remove_effect = {
			514 = {
				set_state_flag = algeria_oil_wells_completed_1
			}
			514 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 15
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	algeria_oil_wells_2 = { #499

		icon = oil

		allowed = {

		}

		
		available = {
			owns_state = 514
			controls_state = 514

		}

		}

		visible = {
			514 = { has_state_flag = algeria_oil_wells_completed_1 }
			owns_state = 514
			controls_state = 514	
			NOT = {
				514 = { has_state_flag = algeria_oil_wells_completed_2 }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 120

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {  # Too low PP
				factor = 0.5
					has_political_power < 80
			}
			modifier = { #We have plenty of PP, avanti!
				factor = 3
				has_political_power > 200
			}
			modifier = { #Running out of the stuff, need more!
				factor = 5
				has_resources_in_country = {
					resource = oil
					amount < 1
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			514 = {
				set_state_flag = algeria_oil_wells_completed_2
			}
			514 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 15
				}
			}
		}

		allowed = {

		}
		
		available = {
			owns_state = 522
			controls_state = 522
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2
			has_tech = excavation8
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 522
			}
		}

		visible = {
			522 = { has_state_flag = australian_steel_completed_3 }
			owns_state = 522
			controls_state = 522	
			NOT = {
				522 = { has_state_flag = australian_steel_completed_4 }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 120

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {  # Too low PP
				factor = 0.5
					has_political_power < 80
			}
			modifier = { #We have plenty of PP, avanti!
				factor = 3
				has_political_power > 200
			}
			modifier = { #Running out of the stuff, need more!
				factor = 5
				has_resources_in_country = {
					resource = steel
					amount < 1
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			522 = {
				set_state_flag = australian_steel_completed_4
			}
			522 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

		available = {
			owns_state = 563
			controls_state = 563
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2
			has_tech = excavation7
			563 = {
				infrastructure > 1
			}
		}
				
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 563
			}
		}

		visible = {
			563 = { has_state_flag = bystrinskoe_tungsten_6_developed }
			NOT = {
				563 = { has_state_flag = bystrinskoe_tungsten_7_developed }
			}
			controls_state = 563
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 120

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {  # Too low PP
				factor = 0.5
					has_political_power < 80
			}
			modifier = { #We have plenty of PP, avanti!
				factor = 3
				has_political_power > 200
			}
			modifier = { #Running out of the stuff, need more!
				factor = 5
				has_resources_in_country = {
					resource = tungsten
					amount < 1
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			563 = {
				set_state_flag = bystrinskoe_tungsten_7_developed
			}
			563 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten
					amount = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
